<div id="review_1422367999" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1422367999" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1422367999?book_show_action=true">Oct 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=paranormal-uf">paranormal-uf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=actiony">actiony</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1422367999" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13237308596998813117"><b>FANTASTIC! I loved it!<br/><br/>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Book number 9 in the <i>Immortals After Dark</i> series is full of all of the action, humour, romance, and sexy times; and general paranormal badassery that I love about these books.<br/><br/>This time, it’s shifter Garreth MacRieve and Valkyrie, Lucia the Huntress. The timing of this book takes us way back to the beginning of the series, with Garreth stepping in for his missing brother as King of the lycae. He is in New Orleans when he sees Lucia for the first time and his instinc</span>
  <span id="freeText13237308596998813117" style="display:none"><b>FANTASTIC! I loved it!<br /><br />4.5 stars</b><br /><br />Book number 9 in the <i>Immortals After Dark</i> series is full of all of the action, humour, romance, and sexy times; and general paranormal badassery that I love about these books.<br /><br />This time, it’s shifter Garreth MacRieve and Valkyrie, Lucia the Huntress. The timing of this book takes us way back to the beginning of the series, with Garreth stepping in for his missing brother as King of the lycae. He is in New Orleans when he sees Lucia for the first time and his instincts flare with the knowledge that she is his mate – the female that is made for him, and the one that he has waited centuries for.<br /><br />Lucia is another sassy, smart-mouthed and utterly kickass Valkyrie. After a bad decision in her teen years left her dying, she made a deal with a goddess to save her life - in return she would become the greatest archer in the world, as long as she keep herself pure and away from any and all contact with men.<br /><br />These two are a sensational match. From the first moment they are both clearly desperate for each other, and with Garreth determined to claim Lucia, and just as determined to stay away, it sets up an epic battle of wills. The chase goes on for years until the ever-fabulous Nix becomes involved, and Lucia finds herself on a mission in the Amazon to track down a weapon that will kill her greatest enemy, and Garreth just happens to be along for the ride. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“You're my woman, Lousha. Damn you, I'll never want another!”</i>
</blockquote><br />Like other books in the series, Lucia and Garreth don’t have an easy time coming together, but the slow build is fantastic. Their relationship is full of anger, frustration, teasing, and mountains of pent-up-lust, and I loved watching them play off against each other. It’s humorously angsty and full of hotness as they get closer and closer, but not quite, and the tension builds fantastically.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>With his harsh, beast like voice, he rasped, “Woman, you are everything to me!” He wrapped her hair around his fist, forcing her to meet his frenzied gaze. “Why can I no' be that for you? Let me claim you for my own. Choose me this night.”</i>
</blockquote><br />And intermingled with it all is the story of Lucia’s desperate, dangerous and exciting hunt for a mystical weapon that atone for her past and free her from everything that is holding her back from a life with Garreth. <br /><br />I loved this book! It was a fantastic adventure from start to finish. I love Garreth’s relentless pursuit, I love that Lucia gave as much as she could while still holding onto herself, and I love that when they eventually took that final step, they were an absolutely kickass couple determined to fight for each other. And the romantic and action storylines build to a fantastic ending that had me desperate to see how it was all going to work out. <br /><br />There’s a nice tie-in with other books in the series, particularly with Lachlain and Emma’s story, and a lead in to future books with Regin getting quite a bit of story time, and OMG, I love Lucia and Regin together! A little bit wild and absolutely hilarious, I adored their constant banter and teasing. So freaking funny!<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Screw you and the werewolf you rode in on!”</i>
</blockquote><br />This series is so much fun! I love knowing that when start one of these books I’m in for a great time, and this one was no exception. With the audiobook again brilliantly narrated by Robert Petkoff, I was lost in the Kresley Cole’s paranormal world, and loved every moment of Garreth and Lucia’s story.<br /><br />4.5 stars. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13237308596998813117" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_78542762" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/78542762" />
    <a title="Eastofoz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/939365-eastofoz"><img alt="Eastofoz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1203907098p2/939365.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/78542762?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eastofoz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eastofoz" href="/user/show/939365-eastofoz">Eastofoz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">IAD fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/939365-eastofoz?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer78542762" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11409675905882608310">Finally Cole puts out something decent again in her IAD series! It’s been a while and for me anyway the last few stories have been mediocre at best. If you like heroes with accents –and she did a fabulous job with Bowen and Cade’s stories— then you’ll love Garreth. You can’t hear his sexy Scottish brogue as much as you could Bowen’s I thought but she still does an excellent job and very few authors manage to do that well.<br/><br/>So there are two great main characters: Lucia the world’s best archer Valky</span>
  <span id="freeText11409675905882608310" style="display:none">Finally Cole puts out something decent again in her IAD series! It’s been a while and for me anyway the last few stories have been mediocre at best. If you like heroes with accents –and she did a fabulous job with Bowen and Cade’s stories— then you’ll love Garreth. You can’t hear his sexy Scottish brogue as much as you could Bowen’s I thought but she still does an excellent job and very few authors manage to do that well.<br /><br />So there are two great main characters: Lucia the world’s best archer Valkyrie and Garreth the lady’s man Lykae. She’s sworn a vow of chastity and he’s into doing just the opposite; together they make for a fantastic pair ;-) Garreth gradually wins her over and it’s that slow character development that sucks the reader in. You feel them push and pull at each other especially with Garreth’s determination to get her (he chases her to the ends of the earth forever practically) but no matter how much he wants Lucia he respects that he can’t have her sexually as hard as it is for him –and she certainly doesn’t help matters at times. That of course doesn’t stop them from testing the limits but you certainly feel their “frustration”. The steam is very “vivid” and mighty good 8-) The tension building throughout the novel and when the h/h finally give in (because you know they will) will no doubt leave you trying to catch your breath ;-) It’s also a really good love story.<br /><br />The book has Cole’s trademark biting humor (Regin and her texting is a riot!) and banter, very nasty (icky even) villain and lots of strange-o Loreans. Nice to see the return of a lot of former characters and for once Nïx didn’t get on my nerves with her weirdness. She was hilarious! Mari was somewhat annoying but I haven’t really liked her cutthroat business tactics since her book. You should probably read the first three full-length books in the series before this one if you’re not one for spoilers and it helps to know who these past characters are but you won’t necessarily be lost if you don’t. <br /><br />The book didn’t make a 5 star read for me because towards the end of the novel it was getting a little too “Indiana Jones and the Temple of Doom” which detracted from the romance. I also didn’t enjoy the abrupt ending with Garreth and Lucia or the cliffhanger epilogue –that kind of stuff just bugs me because it’s unfulfilling and you’re left hanging. It’s still a good book and I really hope that her next one is along the same lines or better and that she doesn’t go back to the more blah stories like Conrad’s or Murdoch’s. This is up there with the other good ones that make you feel like you have to slow down when you’re reading because you suddenly realize that you’re almost done and the book is just too good to actually end :)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11409675905882608310" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=kick-ass-heroine">kick-ass-heroine</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer470652819" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2457215678725153132"><b>4 All for Garreth stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403392849i/10088104._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Nothing good ever came easy..."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Well Garreth hon, be prepared because Lucia is determined to make it as hard as it can get.<br/><br/>I like this book, just as I like most of KC's books but there was something about Lucia that rubbed me the wrong way. I didn't hate her but she did irritate me a lot at times. She protested too much, resisted too much. I like heroines who go after what they want(like most of the other Valkyries do) and Lucia saw what she wanted and ran the other wa</span>
  <span id="freeText2457215678725153132" style="display:none"><b>4 All for Garreth stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403392849i/10088104._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Nothing good ever came easy..."</i>
</b><br><br>Well Garreth hon, be prepared because Lucia is determined to make it as hard as it can get.<br><br>I like this book, just as I like most of KC's books but there was something about Lucia that rubbed me the wrong way. I didn't hate her but she did irritate me a lot at times. She protested too much, resisted too much. I like heroines who go after what they want(like most of the other Valkyries do) and Lucia saw what she wanted and ran the other way.<br><br><b>
  <i>“If I have to scour the entire earth, I'll hunt her down. I will no' falter. One day I will bring my female back to my home - back to my bed...She was born to be found by me.” </i>
</b><br><br>I do love Garreth. I liked how he never gave up, I loved how he remained hopeful and determined despite all the shit Lucia put him through. He is also a Lykae which doesn't hurt. They're definitely my favourite male race in IAD's. My female is Valkyries.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Have you ever fought an opponent you had no defense against? Like a fire breather or an acid spitter?"<br>"Once I faced a female with diamond skin," Nix said breathlessly. "I was transfixed - even as she was choking the life out of me."<br>"Really?"<br>"No, I saw that character on X-Men. I just wanted to commiserate. Alas, I have no weaknesses.”<br><br><br>“This is what it's all been about with you," he said in an even tone. "All the fear, all<br>the running. The nightmares." When she nodded, he said, "You called him the devil."<br>"He is." What are you thinking, Scot?<br>"But you... married him?"<br>MacRieve's disgusted with me. "Basically? Yes."<br>"Ceremony and everything?"<br>She swallowed. "He tricked me into it. I-I was only sixteen."<br>A muscle ticked in his cheek and his irises grew pale. "Then know this..."<br>She stopped breathing.<br>"Lass, I'm about to make you a widow--” <br><br>“She took me to a mall yesterday"' Lachlain sounded as if he'd just stifled a shudder. "And she pointed to a boy and said, 'I think I want one.' So naturally, I start thinking, Where can I get a wee mortal? But she meant a bairn—our bairn.”</i>
</b><br><br><br><i>Re-read it as part of the IAD series Read-A-Long with the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/100383-league-of-lusty-ladies" rel="nofollow noopener">League of Lusty Ladies</a>.</i></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1900499282" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9275643731848252478">5 Electric Stars.... This is absolutely one of my favorite books in the series... focusing on the Dark Lykae Prince, Garreth MacRieve, and his Valkyrie mate "The Archer", Lucia, as they traverse the dangerous and mystical Amazon seeking a diemort (god killer) in order to avoid a pending apocalypse... a powerful storyline, off the charts chemistry, action packed sequences, and a stunning backdrop culminate to bring forth an enticing and captivating story that I could not put down... the MacRieve </span>
  <span id="freeText9275643731848252478" style="display:none">5 Electric Stars.... This is absolutely one of my favorite books in the series... focusing on the Dark Lykae Prince, Garreth MacRieve, and his Valkyrie mate "The Archer", Lucia, as they traverse the dangerous and mystical Amazon seeking a diemort (god killer) in order to avoid a pending apocalypse... a powerful storyline, off the charts chemistry, action packed sequences, and a stunning backdrop culminate to bring forth an enticing and captivating story that I could not put down... the MacRieve family is by far my favorite clan in the series with their Scottish brogue, protective natures, and unending charm they are the epitome of sexy, alpha male... add into the equation the Valkyrie with their ancient powers, warrior personalities, and insane humor and you have a lethal combination that causes explosive chemistry... Garreth and Lucia certainly fit these molds and brought forth a sultry, witty, and entertaining pairing that held me spellbound... a fantastic read from start to finish creating an enticing storyline to continue through the series...highly anticipating the next read:)</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1561936339" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9585005494762250875">Garreth MacRieve, Prince of the Lykae<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463405442i/19114527._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Lucia the Huntress<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465521981i/19368573._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>This series is a lot of fun. There are no love triangles and no cheating. Not that I've read, so far. <br/>Garreth. Oh my goodness!! Lykae Prince. Super hot! Not only are they immortal, but they are extremely good-looking. Lucky! He is my favorite Lykae so far. Nothing gets him down. He is a sweetie. He did have one breaking point, but that didn't last long. <br/>Lucia. Huntress. I actually liked her. Usually, the heroines in this series are pretty bi</span>
  <span id="freeText9585005494762250875" style="display:none">Garreth MacRieve, Prince of the Lykae<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463405442i/19114527._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Lucia the Huntress<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465521981i/19368573._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This series is a lot of fun. There are no love triangles and no cheating. Not that I've read, so far. <br>Garreth. Oh my goodness!! Lykae Prince. Super hot! Not only are they immortal, but they are extremely good-looking. Lucky! He is my favorite Lykae so far. Nothing gets him down. He is a sweetie. He did have one breaking point, but that didn't last long. <br>Lucia. Huntress. I actually liked her. Usually, the heroines in this series are pretty bitchy. But, in a tolerable way. Lucia had one episode and got hysterical at Garreth, which upset me, but that didn't last long either. <br>Kresley Cole is really good at writing dialogue between partners. But, I'd like to know more about the characters. Incorporate their likes and dislikes. What separates one Lykae from the next? They are all big, attractive, possessive, protective, fierce etc. What hobbies are they into. They've lived a really long time. The women in these stories tend to get a greater depth in character, which is good.<br>The men are just hot! Do I really have a problem with that. Nope. I'm going to read the next book now. Bye:) </span>

<div id="review_286006256" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/286006256" />
    <a title="Jane Stewart" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3789528-jane-stewart"><img alt="Jane Stewart" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1346001994p2/3789528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/286006256?book_show_action=true">Feb 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jane Stewart" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jane Stewart" href="/user/show/3789528-jane-stewart">Jane Stewart</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3789528-jane-stewart?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer286006256" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13272583344514889409">Not good. Not fun. All the conflict is based on the heroine keeping secrets from the hero which she doesn’t need to keep.<br/><br/>STORY BRIEF:<br/>The Valkyrie Lucia was captured by the evil demon Crom. She escaped but was near death. The goddess Skathi brought her back to life and gave her great archery skills. Lucia was told she must never have sex or she would lose these skills. Crom has been imprisoned but is about to break free. If he does, he will cause an apocalypse. Crom controls people’s minds. Lucia</span>
  <span id="freeText13272583344514889409" style="display:none">Not good. Not fun. All the conflict is based on the heroine keeping secrets from the hero which she doesn’t need to keep.<br /><br />STORY BRIEF:<br />The Valkyrie Lucia was captured by the evil demon Crom. She escaped but was near death. The goddess Skathi brought her back to life and gave her great archery skills. Lucia was told she must never have sex or she would lose these skills. Crom has been imprisoned but is about to break free. If he does, he will cause an apocalypse. Crom controls people’s minds. Lucia is the only creature immune to him, which means she is the only one who can get close enough to kill him. So she goes on a quest to get a magic arrow which she will use to kill Crom. Unfortunately she meets Lykae (wolf-shifter) Garreth. He has been waiting to find his mate for a thousand years, and it’s Lucia. He follows her, chases her, protects her, and wants to have sex with her.<br /><br />REVIEWER’S OPINION:<br />The major sources of conflict between the couple was Lucia keeping secrets from Garreth. She didn’t need to keep those secrets. But there would be no story if she told him the truth. I was so disappointed. This was not enjoyable. He wants to have sex with her, but she doesn’t tell him that if she has sex, she will lose her archery skills and then be unable to kill Crom which will cause an apocalypse. Instead she keeps saying “no sex.” But he’s confused. He knows she wants sex; he can smell her arousal. And then she repeatedly runs away from him through most of the book. Later when he discovers she plans to kill Crom, he goes with her. Does she tell him about Crom’s mind control abilities and that she is immune? No. So more bad things happen. I was so annoyed that the relationship conflicts were based on her keeping secrets. Sure there were a few other conflicts like being attacked by large creatures and bad guys. But those were more like generic-filler attack and fight scenes.<br /><br />I had another problem with the psychic Nix. This happens too much in weak fiction. A psychic gives the heroine clues and hints about what to do or where to go, but the psychic doesn’t answer all the questions which creates “more mystery.” Whenever the plot needs to be moved, the psychic comes along and says do this now. It’s a weak plot device.<br /><br />There were two good things. The author has a fun style with the occasional snappy, hip dialogue. Also, there were some good hot sex scenes. Garreth’s hotness was the typical Lykae desire to please his mate, protect her, and do things for her - which is irresistible.<br /><br />OTHER BOOKS:<br />The author has more than a dozen books in this series “Immortals After Dark.” My favorite is “A Hunger Like No Other.” I also liked “If You Deceive” from the MacCarrick Brothers series.<br /><br />DATA:<br />Story length: 431 pages. Swearing language: strong, including religious swear words. Sexual language: strong. Number of sex scenes: 7. Total number of sex scene pages: 30. Setting: present day New Orleans area, the Amazon, and Scotland. Copyright: 2010. Genre: paranormal romance.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13272583344514889409" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_73398628" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/73398628" />
    <a title="Mel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2295424-mel"><img alt="Mel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1305638929p2/2295424.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/73398628?book_show_action=true">Oct 04, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mel" href="/user/show/2295424-mel">Mel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2295424-mel?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer73398628" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5137873106728022596">Pleasure of a Dark Prince is the 9th in the Immortal After Darker series and – at the risk of sounding repetitive- Kresley Cole does not disappoint. The book was another fun and engaging read and a great addition to an already great series.<br/><br/>This time we see werewolf Garreth MacRieve and Valkyrie Lucia the Archer slowly but surely fall in love. Actually, the ‘slowly and surely’ part more goes for Lucia. Cause Garreth is in love the very moment he spots Lucia. She is his mate, he knows it, he feels</span>
  <span id="freeText5137873106728022596" style="display:none">Pleasure of a Dark Prince is the 9th in the Immortal After Darker series and – at the risk of sounding repetitive- Kresley Cole does not disappoint. The book was another fun and engaging read and a great addition to an already great series.<br /><br />This time we see werewolf Garreth MacRieve and Valkyrie Lucia the Archer slowly but surely fall in love. Actually, the ‘slowly and surely’ part more goes for Lucia. Cause Garreth is in love the very moment he spots Lucia. She is his mate, he knows it, he feels it and he is ready to serve and protect from that moment on! Lucia can’t deny she’s attracted to Garreth but she cannot afford to fall in love and/or have sex as her arching abilities are connected to her chastity vow. So… she runs. <br />Garreth, determined not to repeat his brother’s (Lachlain) or his nephew’s (Bowen) mistakes of overcrowding and hurting their mates, lets her run. But ofcourse he’s sure to follow her. This while protecting her from attempts to her life and trying to dodge attempts by Lucia and her BFF Regin, to slow him down… with avalanches and major explosions and all that. But Garreth is a Lykae who just found his mate, in other words: he is an <i>obsessed</i> man on a mission and nothing can stop him from following Lucia to (literally) the end of the world. <br /><br />I really liked this book. It was a combination of the books of Lachlain, Bowen and Sebastian. There was a big adventure part, the sexual tension was apparent throughout the story and the love scenes were sizzling! There were a few very romantic and touching parts and many laugh out loud moments. <br />The book starts in the same time frame as IAD #2 (Lachlain &amp; Emma). This means we see a few past events, this time through different perspectives. This revisiting of older events was fresh in Conrad’s book, exciting in Murdoch’s book but almost felt repetitive in this book. Just as I was thinking it got a bit boring, Cole did something completely different: we went a year ahead in time. This was great because times have changed and the Accession has started!<br />I liked Lucia but not as much as I thought I would. She was very ‘human’, had her faults, doubts and insecurities. But I did think she made life harder on herself. Also: I didn’t like the fact that she thought nobody would understand her, but didn’t bother to explain herself. It’s called ‘self fulfilling prophecy’, dear Lucia. Anyway, in the end she all made up for it, so I’m loving her now.<br />My big love however is Garreth. Oh Garreth MacRieve! This werewolf was overbearing but patient, adorable but impossible, out of control but tender, he was wonderful!<br /><br />The epilogue sets up the plot for the upcoming three books (coming out this year!). It really leaves you wanting more and I for one can’t wait till the fall of 2010.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5137873106728022596" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3587322973" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3587322973" />
    <a title="Kenzie The Dragon Queen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen"><img alt="Kenzie The Dragon Queen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1575851043p2/42276702.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3587322973?book_show_action=true">Oct 21, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kenzie The Dragon Queen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kenzie The Dragon Queen" href="/user/show/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen">Kenzie The Dragon Queen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/26044682-pleasure-of-a-dark-prince">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of Immortals After Dark, and all Paranormal Romance.</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=supernatural-paranormal">supernatural-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=books-i-have-reviewed">books-i-have-reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3587322973" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4164940121945017019"><b>
  <i>”The apocalypse has already begun, you see. Just a smidgen of Armageddon so far. Still fixable, but not for long. Ticktock.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><br/>This book may be Kresley Cole’s best piece of writing in the entire <i>Immortals After Dark</i> series, so far. With that being said, personal taste, opinions, and preferences will determine how good you find this book to actually be. If you're a fan of different types of archetypes and tropes, that could dictate how enjoyable you find this novel.<br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”I’ll do this to you till t</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText4164940121945017019" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>”The apocalypse has already begun, you see. Just a smidgen of Armageddon so far. Still fixable, but not for long. Ticktock.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />This book may be Kresley Cole’s best piece of writing in the entire <i>Immortals After Dark</i> series, so far. With that being said, personal taste, opinions, and preferences will determine how good you find this book to actually be. If you're a fan of different types of archetypes and tropes, that could dictate how enjoyable you find this novel.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>”I’ll do this to you till there’s something to take the place of your vows—until you see the two of us together as your religion.</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Let me just start off by saying that this book utilized the Chekhov’s gun writing rule adeptly. The technique was used quite simply, but really well throughout the story at multiple occurrences in different ways. It ended up paying off wonderfully. I know that bringing up certain details in the first act, that end up coming full circle in the third act, doesn’t always work for every story. However, it worked very well for this one.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“And on top of everything you have to evade your Lykae.”<br />“I’m not evading him.” I’m totally evading him. “And he’s not my Lykae”.</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />I’ve said it before and I’ll say it again. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4428.Kresley_Cole" title="Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Kresley Cole</a> continues to improve her writing skills with every book, and her ability continually grows with every story she writes. Growth, talent, and dedication to doing better are always traits I admire in authors, and people in general. I will say that the miscommunication trope was technically used. However, it didn't give me the urge to burn down something in a rage the way this trope normally does. For the simple reason, that I completely believe that even if the characters had communicated with each other, the story would have still played out the exact same way, and the characters all but confirm that themselves. So I'm going to let it slide.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>”Basically, you’ll loose your mind, turning animalistic, hunting me down until you claim me repeatedly, biting my neck and marking me as your possession. Nothing will stop you—no cage can hold you. Did I miss anything?”<br />“Aye, Lousha.” His gaze raked over her and his voice deepened. “The fact that you’re going to like it.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />I thought <i>Kresley Cole</i> did a much better job of writing a new story that overlaps with the different ones she wrote years before, in this book, than she did in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26044765.Deep_Kiss_of_Winter__Includes_Immortals_After_Dark___8__Alien_Huntress___3_5_" title="Deep Kiss of Winter (Includes Immortals After Dark, #8; Alien Huntress, #3.5) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Deep Kiss of Winter</a>. Both that story and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26044682.Pleasure_of_a_Dark_Prince__Immortals_After_Dark___9_" title="Pleasure of a Dark Prince (Immortals After Dark, #9) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Pleasure of a Dark Prince</a> start taking place around the very beginning of the series. However, neither book was written or released until many years and books later. In my review of <i>Deep Kiss of Winter</i>, I explained how I thought Cole didn’t write overlapping stories that take place over different periods of time very well. I feel completely different about how she did the exact same thing with this book. I think <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4428.Kresley_Cole" title="Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Kresley Cole</a> quickly learned how to maneuver writing overlapping stories much better in this book. I actually thought she did it so well that I was beginning to think that I actually liked <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25380932.A_Hunger_Like_No_Other__Immortals_After_Dark___2_" title="A Hunger Like No Other (Immortals After Dark, #2) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">A Hunger Like No Other</a> (the book that overlaps with this one) more than I remember enjoying it. Once again, Cole counties to impress with how well she learns, adapts, and improves.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>”I’ll shoot you so full of arrows—“<br />He held her tight. “Eventually, you will run out of those.”<br />“I make my own,” she said between gritted teeth.<br />“O’ course you do. But I consider your archery our foreplay. So—fire—away.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Now, let’s move onto the characters. Our heroine is Lucia The Huntress. A Valkyrie shrouded in mystery, that is simply known for being THE archer. There isn’t a single archer in the world better than her, and she knows it. However, that’s pretty much the only thing anyone could know about her unless they were extremely close to her. Reign The Radiant, Lucia’s best friend and Valkyrie half-sister is the only one that knows Lucia’s dark secrets and mysterious past. And Nïx of course, since she is a soothsayer beyond compare. I thought Lucia was an interesting character caught in a complex and difficult situation. I wouldn’t say that she’s my favorite heroine in the <i>Immortals After Dark</i> series, but she’s definitely not my least favorite. I'd say she probably lands somewhere in the middle. I’ve always thought that Kresley Cole has had a surprising knack for making all her main characters and side characters especially compelling and interesting. I think that’s part of what makes it so easy to quickly latch onto a side character that’s introduced in one installment, and made into a main character in the next. You have to be good at making characters likable and intriguing if you want your audience to get excited about a minor character in a previous book becoming a main character in the next book.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>”The great evil... Ringing a bell?”<br />“We’ll worry about that later,” Nïx said. “For now, let’s stop at least one apocalypse. Aren’t you on the books for an attempted assassination soon? Where is that Post-it...?”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />So, now let’s talk about our hero, Garreth MacRieve. Holy hot heck, I LOVED him! Where do I start? Okay, let me start by saying that he’s sex on a stick hot, and super sexy in that ultra-masculine aggressive alpha type of way. However, he was also so much more considerate and emotionally intelligent than a lot of the previous male main characters in the series. He managed to exude this rough cocky masculine energy, while still being receptive and patient towards Lucia’s boundaries. Also, I feel it's important to note that he doesn’t just seem like a guy that lands in the middle of the spectrum between these two archetypes. He managed to be both at the same time, and I think that’s what makes him so alluring and likable. He was so sexy and alpha-like, that Lucia lots all cohesive thought to lust, to the point that she was sure his demeanor towards her meant she was his mate. While also simultaneously being so mindful and respectful of her, that Lucia then thought she couldn’t possibly be his mate, because if she were, he wouldn’t be so patient. I truly loved his character. He was just the right blend of all the best traits.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>”He’d told her that she wasn’t his mate, but she thought he’d lied since his reaction had been so fierce. Now she began to believe again, because otherwise he’d have been thumping his chest and snarling, “Mine!” as he slung her over his shoulder.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Outside of the two main characters, there were also great side characters, that if you’ve read this series in chronological order, you already know. Heck, even one of the villains was a previously introduced character (but I won’t say who, because that’s a spoiler). As always, I was delighted to read about Reign and Nïx being apart of this book! They are two of my all-time favorite characters in this universe. This book fleshes out Reign’s origins a bit more since they are intertwined in Lucia’s as well. Lachlain is also in the story, usually to support his brother. He was actually so understanding and attentive with his brother, that I may have to reevaluate how I feel about his character. I really appreciated that Kresley Cole put emphasis on Garreth and Lachlain’s brotherly relationship, as well as Lucia and Reign’s sisterly one. So often in romance novels, I feel like all other relationships and friendships are too easily dismissed when compared to the “epic love” between the main characters. Not so much in this case though. The Lykae truly are like wolves, in the way that their pack is their family. And their family, in this case, is a clan (I’m starting to understand why it makes sense for them to be Scottish now). Even Lucia states that as children she and Reign dreamed of living in mansions next door to each other when they grew up. A thousand years later, Lucia hasn’t really budged on that.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>”You’ve never seen a creature shoot as she—“<br />“I have a good idea.” Lachlain drew his shirt aside, exposing a wound on his shoulder.<br />I’ll bluidy kill her. She went to Scotland and shot my brother!”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />I liked Lucia and Garreth's relationship together, and how sex played a lesser role in them falling in love. I haven’t encountered a story of Cole’s that’s done that since <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25550785.Dark_Needs_at_Night_s_Edge__Immortals_After_Dark___5_" title="Dark Needs at Night's Edge (Immortals After Dark, #5) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Dark Needs at Night's Edge</a>. With that being said, I think the latter handled the “falling in loving without sex" part, much better because I still felt like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26044682.Pleasure_of_a_Dark_Prince__Immortals_After_Dark___9_" title="Pleasure of a Dark Prince (Immortals After Dark, #9) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Pleasure of a Dark Prince</a> needed a little extra spice. Simply because the structure of the story is so different, which means the romantic aspect requires different factors to flourish properly. With that being said, don’t let what I just wrote deter you from reading this book. The romantic facet really was handled very well. I believe that’s what made this book tug on my heartstrings a little differently than most of the other installments in this series. Something about this love story has something a bit special about it.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>”She feared he was the type of man women got reckless over, made stupid decisions for. He made her think, Vows of chastity? What vows?”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />I think that this book handled the action/adventure piece better than some other books in the series, and it was more cohesive and smoothly written. I feel like that’s an area a lot of romance authors that blend genres struggle with, but Cole is getting a little better with each book. She still struggles with it, but I’d definitely say that she handles writing the overarching plot and action-packed endings against “a great evil” much better than she did before. I still think that area is lacking, but this is a romance novel first, and a paranormal novel second. So I suppose it’s natural for the action/adventure parts to get less attention. Nonetheless, Kresley Cole continues to expand on the magical lore and world-building of the series, and I feel like she does a really good job of handling that aspect. I’m always immersed in her stories by how sleekly she creates and further expands on creative lore for these books.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>”Fine. We can act like fuckups idling about. As per our usual. But if we cap a god, I’m telling everyone I know!”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />All in all, this was a really solid installment in the <i>Immortals After Dark</i> series, that manages to further other stories in this universe, without in any way taking away from the main story of this book. Without spoiling anything, I will say that I was very happy with how Garreth and Lucia’s story concluded. The epilogue also turned out to be an interesting glimpse into the future of the series, that surprised, scared, and excited me at the same time. I’ll definitely continue binge reading this series!<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>”The truth is that I’d rather march into hell with you than bask in heaven without you.”</i>
</b><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4164940121945017019" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('8wTplKlzSV6qeMHhQ9md4c1a4PtHGbE7CeXucpqob1HS7rHWl1o1G7tITfCGfc0/U0IPQPAz9VlJJVyg3nUlYg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vfsRpmbuoMCAkaUXfWzTlz6S83lifebg2d9npXFPF9ecEUnkWMfchZGhKQa4yINJoIocwtVXooKZH9V3NZJd5A==')})
  }
//]]>

<span id="freeTextContainer17917396076291956990">Kresley Cole is the #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author of the electrifying Immortals After Dark paranormal series, the young adult Arcana Chronicles series, the erotic Gamemakers series, and five award-winning historical romances.<br/><br/>A master’s grad and former athlete, she has traveled over much of the world and draws from those experiences to create her memorable characters and settings. <br/>Her IAD bo</span>
  <span id="freeText17917396076291956990" style="display:none">Kresley Cole is the #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author of the electrifying Immortals After Dark paranormal series, the young adult Arcana Chronicles series, the erotic Gamemakers series, and five award-winning historical romances.<br /><br />A master’s grad and former athlete, she has traveled over much of the world and draws from those experiences to create her memorable characters and settings. <br />Her IAD books have been translated into 23 foreign languages, garnered three RITA awards, a RWA Hall of Fame induction, and consistently appear on the bestseller lists, in the U.S. and abroad.<br /><br />Cole lives in Florida with her family. Learn more about Kresley at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.kresleycole.com">www.kresleycole.com</a> &amp; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.thearcanachronicles.com">www.thearcanachronicles.com</a><br /><br /></span>
